Calculation Trail (every step, every number)
Step 1 — Pi Ratings
formula: composite = (home_rating + away_rating) / 2
Spain: home_rating=0.4910, away_rating=-0.0491 → composite = (0.4910 + -0.0491) / 2 = 0.2210 (from 9 matches)
Saudi Arabia: home_rating=-0.5098, away_rating=0.0510 → composite = (-0.5098 + 0.0510) / 2 = -0.2294 (from 7 matches)
Step 2 — Calibration Parameters
total_anchor = 3.0278 (fitted, n=36 2026 matches)
rho = -0.1000 (fitted) — Dixon-Coles low-score correlation
Step 3 — Lambdas (Expected Goals per Team)
formula: margin = home_composite − away_composite
formula: λ_H = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 + margin/2)
formula: λ_A = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 − margin/2)
margin = 0.2210 − -0.2294 = 0.4504
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.0278/2 + 0.4504/2) = 1.7391
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.0278/2 − 0.4504/2) = 1.2887
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.7391, λ_A=1.2887, ρ=-0.1000:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.7391×1.2887×(-0.1000) = 1.2241
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.7391, E[away goals] = 1.2887
Step 5 — Market Derivations (cell summation)
home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.4694
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2569
away_win = Σ P(h,a) for h < a = 0.2737
over_2.5 = Σ P(h,a) for h+a > 2.5 = 0.5830
btts_yes = Σ P(h,a) for h≥1 AND a≥1 = 0.6080

τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

margin = 0.0023 − 0.1311 = -0.1288
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.0278/2 + -0.1288/2) = 1.4495
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.0278/2 − -0.1288/2) = 1.5783
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.4495, λ_A=1.5783, ρ=-0.1000:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.4495×1.5783×(-0.1000) = 1.2288
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.4495, E[away goals] = 1.5783
Step 5 — Market Derivations (cell summation)
home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.3401
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2633
